if(start < 0) return null;

var end=document.cookie.indexOf(';', start);

<div id="O1" class="ng-widget model-highlights-overview " >
<style>
div .overview-skin {
background-image: url(/resources/ford/focus/2014/enhancedhighlights/fcs14_electric_overview.jpg);
}
</style>
<div class="overview-skin">
<div class="text-container left">
<h2>
</h2>
<p>
Powered exclusively by a lithium-ion battery, the 2014 Ford Focus Electric has an EPA-estimated
rating of 110 city MPGe.* The Focus Electric is now available to own at one of our Certified Electric Vehicle (EV) Dealers. Ask your tax advisor to see if you may be eligible for a federal tax credit of up to $7,500 for this vehicle. There may also be state and local
tax incentives.
</p>
<div class="button-container">
<a class="ui-grad ui-grad-blue-s model-button faq-trigger">See the FAQ</a>
</div>
</div>
<div class="disclaimer">
<p>*Actual mileage will vary. MPGe is the EPA equivalent measure of gasoline fuel efficiency for electric mode operation.</p>
</div>
</div>
</div>
<div id="LF1" class="ng-widget model-highlights-largefeature " >
<div class="car large-feature-container right">
<div class="text-container">
<h2>
Enjoy Gas-Free Driving.
</h2>
<p>
The Focus Electric gets all of its power from a state-of-the-art 23 kWh liquid-cooled, lithium-ion battery. It has an EPA-estimated range of 76 gas-free miles on each charge and is engineered to reach a top speed of 84 mph.* The all-electric motor is designed to help
reduce energy loss and heat generation while reducing your carbon footprint.
</p>
<p class="disclaimer">
* Actual mileage will vary.
</p>
</div>
<div class="image-container">
<img src="/resources/ford/focus/2014/enhancedhighlights/fcs14_electric_feat_1.jpg?v=1375160469000" alt="Enjoy Gas-Free Driving." title="Enjoy Gas-Free Driving." />
</div>
<div class="clear"></div>
</div>

<div id="faq" class="ng-widget faq " >
<div id="faq-flip" class="ng-widget group-flip group-flip" >
<div class="flip-make" data-make="Ford"></div>
<div class="buttons">
<a class="close button">Close</a>

<h1><strong>FOCUS </strong> electric FAQ</h1>
<ul class="faq-menu" data-trimname="Electric">
<li data-cid="C1">THE BASICS</li>
<li data-cid="C2">DRIVING</li>
<li data-cid="C3">CHARGING</li>
<li data-cid="C4">TECHNOLOGY</li>
<li data-cid="C5">OPERATING COST</li>
<li data-cid="C6">ORDERING</li>
</ul>
<div class="faq-container">
<div data-cid="C1" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q1">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How is the Focus Electric different from the Toyota Prius (or a typical hybrid)?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric is an all-electric vehicle. Unlike typical hybrid vehicles, there is no gas engine that kicks in to supply additional power. All the power is supplied by the lithium-ion battery system and electric motor. No gas is ever needed.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q2">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>What does MPGe mean?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
MPGe stands for miles per gallon equivalent. It’s the EPA’s method for comparing the relative efficiency of all-electric and plug-in hybrid electric vehicles to conventional gas-powered vehicles. The EPA’s formula equates one gallon of gasoline to 33.7 kilowatt-hours of electricity.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q3">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>What company supplies the vehicle’s lithium-ion batteries?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Compact Power, Inc. (CPI), based in Troy, MI, is the supplier of the lithium-ion battery packs for Focus Electric.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q4">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Where is the Focus Electric built?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric is built at the Michigan Assembly Plant in Wayne, Michigan – right alongside the gas-powered Focus. Michigan Assembly produces a gas engine vehicle, hybrid, plug-in hybrid, and an all – electric vehicle allowing Ford to be responsive to consumer demand.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q5">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Is the Focus Electric available with automatic or manual transmission?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Focus Electric features a standard, single-speed automatic transmission designed specifically to handle the high rpm range of an electric motor. A manual transmission isn’t practical with such a system.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
<div data-cid="C2" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q6">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How many miles can I go on a charge?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Depending on your driving conditions, Focus Electric can go up to 76 miles on a single charge.*
<div class="disclaimer">*EPA-estimated. Actual mileage will vary.</div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q7">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How fast can I go?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
More than fast enough for most major highways/freeways. The Focus Electric can achieve a top speed of 84 mph.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q8">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Does my battery drain when I’m sitting still?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The electric motor does not draw current while the vehicle is sitting still. But other electrical systems in the vehicle (such as the radio, climate control, interior/exterior lighting) will draw current if they’re left on.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q9">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Can my driving habits improve my MPGe? </p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
As with a conventional gas-powered vehicle, how you drive has a big effect on efficiency. Accelerate slowly. Drive at a steady, moderate speed. And always try to avoid quick/hard braking. The Focus Electric includes numerous features to help, including a Brake Coach feature that helps you track your braking efficiency. The Navigation System’s EcoRoute option also calculates the most efficient route to your destination.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q10">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>What happens if the battery runs out while I’m on the road?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric is equipped with numerous features to help you keep track of and maximize your range. So depleting your battery should, with normal driving, be avoidable.
<br/>
But in extraordinary situations, if your battery should run out before reaching a destination, 24-Hour Roadside Assistance will tow eligible Focus Electric vehicles to the nearest qualified Ford or Lincoln Dealership. At your request, it can also be transported to your home if it is located within 35 miles of the disablement location.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q11">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>The Focus Electric has no spare tire. What if I get a flat?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Focus Electric comes standard with a Tire Mobility Kit that consists of a sealing compound in a canister that will effectively seal most punctures caused by nails or similar objects, along with an air compressor to reinflate the tire. This kit provides a temporary seal allowing you to drive up to 120 miles at a max speed of 50 mph.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
<div data-cid="C3" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q12">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How often should I plug it in?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
For daily driving, you’ll want to plug it in every night.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q13">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How long does it take to charge?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
With the available Leviton 240V charging station, Focus Electric can fully charge in about four hours.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q14">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>I want the 240V charging system installed. What tools/skills do I need to install the charger?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Ford has teamed up with Leviton and AeroVironment, a leading producer of electrical devices, to develop the 240V home charging station compatible with Focus Electric and all upcoming Ford plug-in vehicles. Installing it yourself is not recommended.
<br/><br/>
Instead, the best place to start when preparing your home for an electric vehicle is at your Ford Certified EV Dealer. AeroVironment can provide full service installation or allow consumers to purchase both the Ford-branded Leviton and AeroVironment 240V charging stations without installation.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q15">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>How much does this charging station cost?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Based on current plans, the Leviton 240V home charging station is $849 and the AeroVironment is $899. The average cost for standard installation is expected to retail for approximately $1,799. However, this price can vary depending on your house and garage electrical system. The unit can be purchased along with your Focus Electric through your Ford Certified EV Dealer.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q16">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Where else can I recharge?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
With the included 120V convenience cord, you can recharge the Focus Electric anywhere you can find a standard, dedicated, three-prong outlet. But for faster charging, you can use the MyFord<sup>&#174;</sup> Mobile app to locate the nearest 240V charging stations in your area (or in the area where you may be traveling).
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
<div data-cid="C4" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q17">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Where are the batteries located? Do they take up a lot of the hatch space? </p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric battery pack is located at the rear of the vehicle, under the rear passenger seat and extending into the cargo area. While the battery does take up a portion of the cargo area, the Focus Electric comes standard with a unique Cargo Management System to help make the most of the space available.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q18">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Is it true that the Focus Electric has no fluids like coolant, transmission, steering, brake, etc.?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Not entirely. Focus Electric does use some fluids (including a liquid coolant in the battery system, brake fluid and windshield wiper fluid). However, the Focus Electric will never require an oil change and, most importantly, uses absolutely no gasoline.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q19">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>What can cause my EV range to vary?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Many factors can affect it: ambient temperature, traffic conditions, terrain, driving behavior, use of the vehicle’s climate control system, number and weight of passengers in the car and weight of cargo. That’s why the Focus Electric comes standard with numerous features to help you maximize your range, including cabin preconditioning, which allows you to preheat or precool the cabin while the vehicle is still plugged in to avoid drawing energy from the battery.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q20">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>What are the specifications of the Focus Electric?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Here are some of the basics: <br/>
• Engine: 107 kW electric motor <br/>
• Battery: 23 kWh liquid-cooled lithium-ion battery system <br/>
• Onboard charger: 6.6 kW <br/>
• Transmission: 1-speed automatic <br/>
• Top speed: 84 mph <br/>
• Brakes: 4-wheel disc brake system with Regenerative Braking System <br/>
• Front-wheel drive <br/>
• 5-passenger <br/>
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
<div data-cid="C5" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q21">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Will the Focus Electric qualify for a federal tax incentive?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric may be eligible for a federal tax credit of up to $7,500. Information on federal income tax credit rules and regulations can be found here: <i>http://www.fueleconomy.gov/feg/taxevb.shtml</i>.
<br/><br/>
Additional information on federal, state and local incentives and laws can be found here: <i>http://www.afdc.energy.gov/afdc/laws/</i>.
<br/><br/>
You can also consult your tax advisor for details.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q22">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Will maintenance costs be more or less than for a similar gas engine vehicle?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
With fewer moving mechanical parts than a conventional gas-powered vehicle, scheduled maintenance is nearly eliminated. In fact, scheduled Multi-Point Inspections, checking the tire pressure, rotating the tires and filling the windshield washer fluid are about all you’ll ever need to do.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q23">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Is there a more economical way to charge the Focus Electric?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
To take advantage of lower off-peak-hour utility rates, the MyFord<sup>&#174;</sup> Mobile app and Web portal let you customize your charging schedule. This allows your Focus Electric to charge during times when electricity prices are lowest.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
<div data-cid="C6" class="faq-category-content">
<ul>
<li data-question="Q24">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Where is the Focus Electric available?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
Ford Certified EV dealers are located nationwide and are able to sell Ford’s plug-in products: Focus Electric, C-MAX Energi, and Fusion Energi.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
<li data-question="Q25">
<div class="faq-question">
<span class="action-button"></span>
<p>Where will the vehicle be shipped?</p>
</div>
<div class="faq-answer">
The Focus Electric can be shipped to any of the EV Certified Dealers; please use the locate a dealer tool advanced search by selecting ‘Electric vehicles’ to find a dealership where a Ford plug-in can be shipped.
<div class="disclaimer"></div>
</div>
</li>
</ul>
</diV>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>
</div>

</a>
</div>
</div>
</div>

<h3>Additional Disclosures</h3>
<dl>
<dt id="disclaimer1">1</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerStartingMSRP">Starting MSRP excludes destination/delivery charge, taxes, title and registration. Optional equipment not included. Starting A, Z and X Plan price is for qualified, eligible customers and excludes document fee, destination/delivery charge. taxes, title and registration. Not all vehicles qualify for A, Z or X Plan.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer2">2</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerMPG">EPA-estimated city/hwy mpg. See fueleconomy.gov for fuel economy of other engine/transmission combinations. Actual mileage will vary. MPGe is the EPA equivalent measure of gasoline fuel efficiency for electric mode operation.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer3">3</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerTowing">When properly equipped.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer4">4</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerOptionPrice">Option/Package price based on Manufacturers Suggest Retail Price excluding taxes based on 5% APR Ford credit financing financed over 60 months. Not all buyers will qualify for Ford Credit financing.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer5">5</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerSellingPrice">The Estimated Selling Price of vehicle less cash back, rebates, and net trade in allowance. It does not include amounts for fees, sales tax, service contracts, etc. Consult your dealer for actual price and complete details.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer6">6</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerAPR">Special APR offers applied to Estimated Selling Price. Special APR offers require Ford Credit Financing. Not all buyers will qualify. See dealer for qualifications and complete details.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer7">7</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerLease">Special Lease offers applied to Estimated Capitalized Cost. Special Lease offers require Ford Credit Financing. Not all buyers will qualify. See dealer for qualifications and complete details.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer8">8</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerLease">See your dealer for details.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer9">9</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerLease">Option/Package price based on A, Z, or X Plan price for qualified, eligible A, Z, or X Plan customers excluding taxes based on 5% APR Ford credit financing financed over 60 months. Not all buyers will qualify for Ford Credit financing.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer15">15</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerClasseTowing">Classes are:  Compact Cars (Fiesta); Small Sedans and Hatchbacks (Focus); Midsize Sedans (Fusion); Full-Size Sedans (Taurus); RWD Sports Cars (Mustang); Small Utilities (Escape); Midsize Utilities (Edge); Large Utilities (Flex and Explorer); Extended Utilities (Expedition); Full-Size Pickups under 8,500 lbs. GVWR, Non-Hybrid (F-150); Full-Size Pickups over 8,500 lbs. GVWR (Super Duty).</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer16">16</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerFuelEconomy">EPA-estimated Fiesta SE with SFE Package; Focus SE with SFE Package. Actual mileage may vary. See fueleconomy.gov for details.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer17">17</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerSyncTouch">Excludes models with SYNC with MyFord Touch.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer18">18</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerEquippedTouch">Only on vehicles equipped with SYNC with MyFord Touch.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer19">19</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerEconomy">See fueleconomy.gov.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer20">20</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerDealerOrders">For Dealer Ordered vehicles, the vehicle has already been ordered by the dealer and is in the process of being manufactured by the factory. If you are interested in the vehicle marked "Dealer Ordered", contact the dealership for a delivery estimate.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer21">21</dt>
<dd id="disclaimer-f-750">On the F-750</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer22">22</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerTowingTests">Based on Ford drive-cycle tests of comparably equipped 2011/2012 Ford and 2011/2012 competitive models. Class is Full-Size Pickups over 8,500 lbs. GVWR.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer27">27</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerSafetyControl">SYNC is available on most Ford vehicles. Features/functionality vary by vehicle/model. Driving while distracted can result in loss of vehicle control. Only use SYNC/MyFord Touch/other devices, even with voice commands, when it is safe to do so. Some features may be locked out while the vehicle is in gear. Traffic alerts and turn-by-turn directions available in select markets. Not all features are compatible with all phones. Message and data rates may apply.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer28">28</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerElectricalSystem">The vehicle's electrical system (including the battery), the wireless service provider's signal and a connected mobile phone must all be available and operating for 911 Assist to function properly. These systems may become damaged in a crash. The paired mobile phone must be connected to SYNC, and the 911 Assist feature enabled, in order for 911 to be dialed. When the feature is ON, 911 Assist uses your paired and connected mobile phone to assist occupants to contact emergency services by dialing 911 if your airbag deploys or, on certain vehicles, if the emergency fuel pump shut-off is activated.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer29">29</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerSubscriptionServices">Complimentary three-year subscription for owners of new vehicles equipped with the service. Subscription fees may apply after three years. Traffic alerts and turn-by-turn directions available in select markets. Message and data rates may apply.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer34">34</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerOptionalSatRadio">Optional. SiriusXM Satellite Radio, Traffic and Travel Link subscriptions sold separately or as a package after trial expires. SiriusXM Traffic and Travel Link service available in select markets. Subscriptions are governed by SiriusXM Customer Agreement; see www.siriusxm.com. Sirius U.S. Satellite Service available in the 48 contiguous states and D.C. Sirius, XM and all related marks and logos are trademarks of Sirius XM Radio Inc.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer36">36</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerOptionalWorkSolutions">Optional Ford Work Solutions. Available on F-Series, E-Series, Transit Connect and Super Duty. Some features unavailable while driving.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer39">39</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerVehicleControl">Remember that even advanced technology cannot overcome the laws of physics. It's always possible to lose control of a vehicle due to inappropriate driver input for the conditions.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer41">41</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerDistractedDriving">911 Assist, VHR, SYNC Services and AppLink not available on Transit Connect. Driving while distracted can result in loss of vehicle control. Only use mobile phones and other devices, even with voice commands, when it is safe to do so.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer42">42</dt>
<dd id="disclaimer-epa-standards">Based on analysis of data published by EPA, 11/10. Actual mileage may vary.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer43">43</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerRegisteredTrademarks">Android is a trademark of Google Inc. iPhone® is a registered trademarks of Apple Inc. The BlackBerry and RIM families of related marks, images and symbols are the exclusive properties and trademarks of Research In Motion Limited.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer48">48</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerBluetoothTrademark">You must have a Bluetooth®-enabled phone paired to your SYNC system. The Bluetooth word mark is a trademark of the Bluetooth SIG, Inc. HD Radio is a proprietary trademark of iBiquity Digital Corp. iPad®, iPod® and iTunes® are registered trademarks of Apple Inc. The term Wi-Fi® is a registered trademark of the Wi-Fi Alliance®. Sony is a registered trademark of the Sony Corporation.</dd>
<dt id="disclaimer49">49</dt>
<dd id="disclaimerVoiceActivatedSync">Only on vehicles with SYNC® with MyFord Touch® with voice activated Navigation system or SYNC with hard drive-based voice activated Navigation system. Commands may vary by model year.</dd>
